class=\"tocnumber\">6</span> <span class=\"toctext\">References</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</div>\n\n<h2><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"About\">About</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a href=\"/rocketleague/index.php?title=Rocket_League_Championship_Series/2021-22/Fall/Sub-Saharan_Africa/1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1\" title=\"Edit section: About\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h2>\n<p><b>RLCS 2021-22 </b> is the second <a href=\"/rocketleague/RLCS\" class=\"mw-redirect\" title=\"RLCS\">RLCS</a> season in 2021, crossing over into 2022. This season introduces the most major changes to the RLCS system yet with more regions and an updated format. 3 splits - Fall, Winter, Spring - each having 3 regional events leading into an international major. Within all these events, each team collected points that determined whether they would qualify for the World Championship or World Championship Wildcard.\n</p>\n<h3><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Broadcast_Talent\">Broadcast Talent</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a href=\"/rocketleague/index.php?title=Rocket_League_Championship_Series/2021-22/Fall/Sub-Saharan_Africa/1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2\" title=\"Edit section: Broadcast Talent\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h3>\n<h4><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Primary_Broadcast\">Primary Broadcast</span><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a href=\"/rocketleague/index.php?title=Rocket_League_Championship_Series/2021-22/Fall/Sub-Saharan_Africa/1&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3\" title=\"Edit section: Primary Broadcast\">edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span></h4>\n<ul><li><b>Host:</b>\n<ul><li><span class=\"flag\"><a href=\"/rocketleague/Category:United_States\"
